< review>
I've been to this location three times. My first experience was not to a standard of which was pleasing. Our waitress was not personable at all, and every time we asked for things that should have been provided like napkins, straws (prior to the plastic straw ban) and drink refills, she gave us a disgusted look like we were bothering her. The different varieties of sushi we ordered were delicious nevertheless. At the suggestion of my husband, we decided to go a second time. Our second experience was a complete turn around, and we were pleasantly delighted with the service we received and there were no issues at all...all of our sushi choices were phenomenal. Our third visit was equally pleasing all around. The ambience of the place is quiet, and the space is not large, just right; the lights have been dimmed all the times I've visited (all visits were at night time). Overall, if you aren't looking for anything extra fancy, you should be pleased with their sushi options.<//review>

106378627413702598943< /UserId.>

< gmapID>
0x80db7e3dec73fea5:0x382ffb282ef09c77</gmapID>
< rate>
1< /rate>
< text>
I give it 1 star b/c the first girl I talked to was actually great.  She was nice!  My husband kept going back and forth on what he wanted engraved via telephone and the woman behind the desk was very understanding and extremely nice - I give her 5 stars!  I went home to get dressed for the get-to-gether (for which I needed the engraved present) and came back to pick up my item.  I stood in line patiently ( I was a waitress for years) and waited my turn.  There were two women off to the side who were being helped and two women in front of me who couldn't decide on which clock they wanted.  Nikki - the customer service representative for the store left the two women on the left and came back to the register to ask the women in front of me if they decided on the clock they wanted.  The women began to discuss back and forth which item they were going to choose.  I figured - hey!  I'm in a hurry; while they wait I'll just grab my item and get out of everyone's hair.  I asked Nikki.  "I'm actually in a hurry; can I just pick up my item really quickly?"

Nikki gave me a very pointed look, a fake smile, and a stare from death and said "i'll be with you in just a moment".  I thought to myself, "okay.....".  She directed her attention back to the women choosing a clock.  Because the women were choosing a clock they were talking amongst themselves.  I waited probably one full minute (while Nikki WATCHED the women talk amongst themselves) and walked around the women to the side of the counter and said again, "I'm really in a hurry - is there any way you can just grab my item really quickly?"

Again - I received the death stare with a sugar coated "I'm helping customers at the moment - I'll be with you as soon as I can"....

I am not used to people (especially customer service representatives from which I am purchasing a high quality item) being pointedly and overtly disgustingly rude to my face and me sitting there and taking it.

At this point, I lost all all regard to Emily Post's guide to manners and told Nikki exactly what her attitude suggested I tell her.  The funny thing is, from the moment I served Nikki exactly what she was serving me, she became much more accommodating (in a very RUDE manner)....

I wanted to PICK UP MY ITEM AND LEAVE THE STORE.  Again, from years of waiting tables and becoming an expert in time management, I KNOW the fastest way to handle a busy store is DO WHAT YOU CAN WHEN YOU CAN and LOSE THE FRIGGIN' ATTITUDE.

I will NEVER go back to this particular store. My husband is  a U.S. Marine and we tend to need a lot of items engraved.  From this point forward I will

1) go 30 miles out of my way to get everything done on base

< review>
What a lovely, locally owned book shop that has something for everyone at a range of price points. Less than a 10 minute walk from the Third Street Promenade!

You can find everything from a $1 sticker to a $4 crystal to a $600 porcelain Buddha. Regardless of your faith or spirituality, there is a vast selection to explore. I love their cook books, yoga instruction books and their children's section.

Excellent selection, fair prices and a kind approach to customer service.

If you're looking to grow your faith, your practice or are looking for spiritual guidance in your life, this is a great place to start.

Pro Tip:
- Skip Amazon and browse for your books here!</review>

< Text>
I have been a frequent customer of Thunderbolt Spiritual Books over the past 7 years, and let me tell you that this place is wonderful. There is something for everyone, and mostly all faiths and forms of spirituality are covered. The downstairs area has an enormous buddah statue where coins and offerings have been left, and it is encircled by small stonesx minerals and crystals that are being sold. There is a larger selection on the left and also kept behind cases to the rear. Along the other wall is a selection of books and tarot cards as well as other tools for divination (runes, healing cards), a selection of prayer beads and bracelets and yoga mats and accessories. Upstairs there are more books and seminars and workshops are held on occasion. They sell a wide range of art; statuettes, tapestries, wall ornaments and pictures to name a few. They also have incense, sage, candles and oils and jewelry made by local artists. All of their staff is extremely knowledgeable and friendly, and Tara the owners' dog is a sweetheart. A place you MUST visit when you are nearby!</Text>

My wife and I fell in love with this place after one visit. First, it's a family ran/owned business. They care about quality over quantity. The food was absolute great and tasted very fresh. <Time>1564524874497< /Time><Rating>2</Rating><gmapID>0x80e9559ac571108b:0x92fd28e3b3a2cc83<//gmapID><user>109785267330252938265</user>< Text>
Great location. Other than that we were not impressed. The server was new, so we will go easy on him. He tried to do a good job. The food though, we expected a better experience. The eggs Benedict was unremarkable, and my wife wondered why there was no hash browns in her breakfast burrito. She said it was bland otherwise. We split a side of biscuits and gravy and didn't finish it because the flavor of rosemary was extremely overpowering in the gravy and the biscuits were doughy, as if undercooked, not light and fluffy as expected. Generally when a place opens, they are still working out the kinks so we will give them another chance after some time. Hopefully they will get their flavors en pointe. This place could go either way. Hopefully it will become another great breakfast location in Solvang.</Text>

<Text>I came to them back in September 2016 when I revived my current daily driver and realized I was in such a rush to get my vehicle up and running, I never left them a review. I will say their current location compared to previous one is much, much nicer, and you definitely won't miss it since it's a corner building. I rarely venture into downtown san jose, I looked at their shop location on Google Maps, found it instantly as soon as I turned off from Bird onto Auzerais.

I will definitely come back again, they've got the best deal around compared to other smog shops that are not gas station smog stations (I don't trust gas stations, just personal preference). I found a Groupon deal for a certain percentage off original price at the last second and they honored the deal, I didn't have to buy it beforehand so that definitely saved me, thanks to them. I had some free time on my hands so I went midday during the week (Thursday afternoon at the time of this posting and had smog check done at noon). I remember Kathy from my first visit, she's a super friendly lady, gave me all the info I needed both over the phone and in person. I think it took around 20-30 minutes, not bad at all considering some places I've been to takes about 45 minutes, and the technician was also incredibly nice and knowledgeable.

I am definitely recommending this place to anyone who lives locally in San Jose and those who are willing to drive out here because they took awesome care of me. Thanks Smog Man!

11/11/20: third time I've had them smog my vehicle now. Superb service as always. As an addition to taking precautions for covid, they have hand sanitizer if you don't have one on you. I'm not sure if they wear gloves but they put seat covers before getting in your car. I was told it would take a hour but I left 45 minutes after handing the keys over. Groupon did have cheaper deals but since I've had them smog my car numerous times in the past, I still came to them as I trust them with my vehicle.
